The location is great. You can see the Songhua River from the room. The Catholic Church is on the right. It is very convenient to walk.
Parking is free. Just register and bind your license plate number. There are ground and underground parking lots.
Breakfast is on the fifth floor. It tastes good and there are many varieties. I especially recommend the beef noodles. It is very flavorful.
Some people say that the facilities are old, but I think it is okay. After all, it has been open for ten years. The decoration style is not very modern or smart, but it looks more flavorful.
Now let me talk about the unsatisfactory parts.
The bed is hard and the pillow is not comfortable. The whole room is very stuffy and the air conditioner is not very useful.
It is said to be a five-star hotel, but there is only a pot of fake green plants in the room. There is no welcome fruit, only two lonely boxes of yogurt.
The most speechless thing is that I checked in on May 13. There was a milk tea cup from May 1 in the cabinet of the room. There were also curly hairs in the bathtub. I was really speechless.
